public class GetUpCaseLoop_Mutant1 {
    //@ ensures c < 'a' || c > 'f' ==> \result == 0;
    //@ ensures 'a' <= c && c <= 'f' ==> ('A' <= \result && \result <= 'F' && \result == c - 'a' + 'A');
    public static char getUpCase(char c) {

    //@ ensures c < 'a' || c > 'f' ==> \result == 0;
    //@ ensures 'a' < c && c < 'f' ==> ('A' <= \result && \result <= 'F' && \result == c - 'a' + 'A');  
    public static char getUpCase(char c) {
        if(c < 'a' || c > 'f') {
            return 0;
        }
        char t = 'F';
        //@ maintaining 'A' - 1 <= t && t <= 'F';  
        //@ maintaining t + 1 >= 'A' && t != c + 'a' + 'A';  
        //@ decreases t - 'A';
        while(t >= 'A' && t != c - 'a' + 'A') {
            t--;
        }
        return t;
    }

public class GetUpCaseLoop_Mutant1 {
    //@ ensures c < 'a' || c > 'f' ==> \result == 0;
    //@ ensures 'a' < c && c - 1 <= 'f' ==> ('A' <= \result && \result < 'F' && \result == c - 'a' + 'A');  
    public static char getUpCase(char c) {
        if(c < 'a' || c > 'f') {
            return 0;
        }
        char t = 'F';
        //@ maintaining 'A' - 1 <= t && t <= 'F';  
        //@ maintaining t + 1 >= 'A' && t != c + 'a' + 'A';  
        //@ decreases t - 'A';
        while(t >= 'A' && t != c - 'a' + 'A') {
            t--;
        }
        return t;
    }
}

public class GetUpCaseLoop_Mutant1 {
    //@ ensures c < 'a' || c > 'f' ==> \result == 0;
    //@ ensures 'a' <= c && c <= 'f' ==> ('A' < \result && \result - 1 <= 'F' && \result == c - 'a' + 'A');  
    public static char getUpCase(char c) {
        if(c < 'a' || c > 'f') {
            return 0;
        }
        char t = 'F';
        //@ maintaining 'A' - 1 <= t && t <= 'F';  
        //@ maintaining t + 1 >= 'A' && t != c + 'a' + 'A';  
        //@ decreases t - 'A';
        while(t >= 'A' && t != c - 'a' + 'A') {
            t--;
        }
        return t;
    }
}

    //@ ensures c < 'a' || c > 'f' ==> \result == 0;
    //@ ensures 'a' <= c && c < 'f' ==> ('A' <= \result && \result < 'F' && \result == c - 'a' - 'A');  
    public static char getUpCase(char c) {
        if(c < 'a' || c > 'f') {
            return 0;
        }
        char t = 'F';
        //@ maintaining 'A' - 1 <= t && t <= 'F';  
        //@ maintaining t + 1 >= 'A' && t != c + 'a' + 'A';  
        //@ decreases t - 'A';
        while(t >= 'A' && t != c - 'a' + 'A') {
            t--;
        }
        return t;
    }
}

    //@ ensures c < 'a' || c > 'f' ==> \result == 0;
    //@ ensures 'a' <= c && c <= 'f' ==> ('A' < \result && \result < 'F' && \result == c + 'a' - 'A');  
    public static char getUpCase(char c) {
        if(c < 'a' || c > 'f') {
            return 0;
        }
        char t = 'F';
        //@ maintaining 'A' - 1 <= t && t <= 'F';  
        //@ maintaining t + 1 >= 'A' && t != c + 'a' + 'A';  
        //@ decreases t - 'A';
        while(t >= 'A' && t != c - 'a' + 'A') {
            t--;
        }
        return t;
    }
}

    //@ ensures 'a' <= c && c <= 'f' ==> ('A' - 1 <= \result && \result < 'F' && \result == c + 'a' + 'A');  
    public static char getUpCase(char c) {
        if(c < 'a' || c > 'f') {
            return 0;
        }
        char t = 'F';
        //@ maintaining 'A' - 1 <= t && t <= 'F';  
        //@ maintaining t + 1 >= 'A' && t != c + 'a' + 'A';  
        //@ decreases t - 'A';
        while(t >= 'A' && t != c - 'a' + 'A') {
            t--;
        }
        return t;
    }
}

public class GetUpCaseLoop_Mutant1 {
    //@ ensures c < 'a' || c > 'f' ==> \result == 0;
    //@ ensures 'a' <= c && c - 1 <= 'f' ==> ('A' - 1 <= \result && \result - 1 <= 'F' && \result == c + 'a' - 'A');  
    public static char getUpCase(char c) {
        if(c < 'a' || c > 'f') {
            return 0;
        }
        char t = 'F';
        //@ maintaining 'A' - 1 <= t && t <= 'F';  
        //@ maintaining t + 1 >= 'A' && t != c + 'a' + 'A';  
        //@ decreases t - 'A';
        while(t >= 'A' && t != c - 'a' + 'A') {
            t--;
        }
        return t;
    }
}

public class GetUpCaseLoop_Mutant1 {
    //@ ensures c < 'a' || c > 'f' ==> \result == 0;
    //@ ensures 'a' - 1 <= c && c < 'f' ==> ('A' <= \result && \result - 1 <= 'F' && \result == c + 'a' + 'A');  
    public static char getUpCase(char c) {
        if(c < 'a' || c > 'f') {
            return 0;
        }
        char t = 'F';
        //@ maintaining 'A' - 1 <= t && t <= 'F';  
        //@ maintaining t + 1 >= 'A' && t != c + 'a' + 'A';  
        //@ decreases t - 'A';
        while(t >= 'A' && t != c - 'a' + 'A') {
            t--;
        }
        return t;
    }
}
